﹛ ﹛ ﹛ ﹛Whenㄛone dayㄛI had thus asked Sangaya of the Belattha clanㄛhe saidㄩ※If
you ask me whether there is another world岸 岸wellㄛif I thought therewereㄛI would say so
﹝But I don't say so﹝And I don't say there neither isㄛnor is notㄛanother world﹝And if you
ask me about the beings producedby chance˙or whether there is any fruitㄛany resultㄛof good
or bad actions˙or whether a man who has won the truth continuesㄛor notㄛafter death岸 岸
